      (plddt): PredictedLDDTHead(
        (layer_norm): LayerNorm(torch.Size([384]), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (linear_1): Linear(in_features=384, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (linear_2): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (act): ReLU()
        (linear_3): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=50, bias=True)
      )
      (distogram): DistogramHead(
        (layer_norm): None
        (linear_in): None
        (act): ReLU()
        (linear): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
      )
      (masked_msa): MaskedMSAHead(
        (layer_norm): None
        (linear_in): None
        (act): ReLU()
        (linear): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=22, bias=True)
      )
      (experimentally_resolved): ExperimentallyResolvedHead(
        (layer_norm): None
        (linear_in): None
        (act): ReLU()
        (linear): Linear(in_features=384, out_features=37, bias=True)
      )
      (pae): PredictedAlignedErrorHead(
        (layer_norm): None
        (linear_in): None
        (act): ReLU()
        (linear): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
      )
    )
  )
)
